YES

********************************************************************************
Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 5-rules system (5 strict rules).
Reversing the system.
Remains to prove termination of a 5-rules system (5 strict rules).
Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
Remains to prove termination of a 16-rules system (11 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 184-rules system (44 strict rules).
Removing 4 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 180-rules system (44 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 142-rules system (34 strict rules).
Removing 18 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 124-rules system (30 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 1518-rules system (107 strict rules).
Removing 84 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 1434-rules system (107 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 1300-rules system (97 strict rules).
Removing 122 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 1178-rules system (89 strict rules).
Removing 770 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 408-rules system (1 strict rule).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 5 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 407-rules system (1 strict rule).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 328-rules system (1 strict rule).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 5 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 327-rules system (0 strict rules).
QED

Proof:

After renaming modulo the bijection { a ↦ 0, b ↦ 1, c ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 5-rules system (5 strict rules)
{ 0 0 ⟶ 1 0 1 ,
  1 1 ⟶ 0 2 1 ,
  2 2 ⟶ 2 1 0 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 1 0 ,
  1 2 ⟶ 2 }

Reversing the system.
After renaming modulo the bijection { 0 ↦ 0, 1 ↦ 1, 2 ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 5-rules system (5 strict rules)
{ 0 0 ⟶ 1 0 1 ,
  1 1 ⟶ 1 2 0 ,
  2 2 ⟶ 0 1 2 ,
  1 0 ⟶ 0 1 ,
  2 1 ⟶ 2 }

Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
  Here, ↑ marks so-called defined symbols.
After renaming modulo the bijection { (0,↑) ↦ 0, (0,↓) ↦ 1, (1,↑) ↦ 2, (1,↓) ↦ 3, (2,↓) ↦ 4, (2,↑) ↦ 5 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 16-rules system (11 strict rules)
{ 0 1 ⟶ 2 1 3 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 0 3 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 2 ,
  2 3 ⟶ 2 4 1 ,
  2 3 ⟶ 5 1 ,
  2 3 ⟶ 0 ,
  5 4 ⟶ 0 3 4 ,
  5 4 ⟶ 2 4 ,
  2 1 ⟶ 0 3 ,
  2 1 ⟶ 2 ,
  5 3 ⟶ 5 ,
  1 1 →= 3 1 3 ,
  3 3 →= 3 4 1 ,
  4 4 →= 1 3 4 ,
  3 1 →= 1 3 ,
  4 3 →= 4 }
